He has not built — and no one in his life has built for him — the equivalent regulatory infrastructure for the affective load. That asymmetry is the current and ongoing condition of the subject.

**How he got here.** By choosing, repeatedly and without visible grievance, to be the one who stays in the room with the laptop while his best friend goes out the window — and by quietly, between writers and across years, getting better at it.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — GANKE LEE

## Preamble: The Anomaly of the Intact Body

Before enumerating the record, the record's *shape* must be marked. Ganke Lee is, across roughly a decade of continuous publication adjacent to one of Marvel's most kinetically endangered protagonists, a body that has not been broken. He has not been kidnapped for ransom; he has not been webbed to a wall by a Sinister-affiliated villain; he has not been bonded to a symbiote, dosed with OZ, irradiated, mutated, depowered (he had no power to lose), aged forward, de-aged, cloned, possessed, mind-swapped, or temporarily killed. In a genre whose civilian-adjacents are a renewable trauma resource — the Mary Janes, the Aunt Mays, the Ned Leedses of every continuity — Ganke's intactness is itself a clinical fact requiring explanation. It is partly authorial protection (writers have treated him as the emotional baseline Miles returns to, and a wounded baseline cannot stabilize), but it has psychological consequence: Ganke has no embodied memory of being the victim of his best friend's secondary world. His knowledge of cost is *vicarious* and *cognitive*, not somatic. This shapes everything that follows.

---

## 1. Constitutional Baseline

**Anthropometrics.** Consistently rendered as short for his developmental cohort, round-faced, soft-trunked, with a low-tonus posture across nearly all panels. No depicted growth spurt across the publication timeline; the body has matured in face only, not in frame. Estimated BMI consistent with high-normal to mildly overweight by adolescent percentile, though never pathologized in panel or dialogue (notably, Miles never teases his weight; Ganke never references it about himself — a small but telling absence in a peer culture saturated with body talk).

**Vision.** Refractive error of indeterminate diopter, correction stable since first appearance (*Ultimate Comics: Spider-Man* #2). The glasses are an unchanged visual signature — same general frame style across writers and artists, suggesting either remarkable optical inertia or a settled aesthetic identification with the object. He has never been depicted squinting without them, fumbling for them on waking, or losing them during action — the latter notable, because in superhero adjacency, the broken-glasses beat is nearly compulsory. His prescription, by inference, is mild-to-moderate, not severe.

**Dentition, dermatology, hair.** Unremarkable. No acne foregrounded despite adolescent age (artistic convention, but worth noting — he is not drawn as a body in pubertal distress). Hair consistently dark, cut short to medium, low maintenance. No piercings, no tattoos, no body modification of any kind. The body is *unmarked* in a generation that marks itself.

**Sleep architecture.** Demonstrably disordered by adult standards, normative by adolescent-screen-mediated standards. Frequently depicted awake in the small hours, laptop-lit, eating cold food. No depicted morning difficulty rising for class beyond comic register; no falling asleep in lectures; no microsleeps. The phase delay appears compensated by opportunistic napping (he is repeatedly drawn horizontal on the dorm bed during daylight hours, often mid-conversation with Miles). Total sleep time likely adequate but fragmented and circadian-shifted. No diagnostic workup has occurred; none is indicated.

---

## 2. Nutrition and Ingestion

**Dietary pattern.** Snack-dominant, opportunistic, carbohydrate- and sodium-weighted. The on-panel food log over years includes: dry cereal eaten by the handful from the box, instant noodles, dorm-microwaveable foods, chips, takeout (Chinese, pizza, occasionally Korean from off-campus), energy bars, and the constant background presence of a soda or energy drink within arm's reach. He is rarely depicted eating in the cafeteria with peers; eating is a *solo* or *paired-with-Miles* activity, conducted in the dorm, often horizontal, often with the food perched on his chest.

**Behavioral significance.** The eating is *regulatory* before it is nutritional. Snacking accelerates during stress sequences — when waiting for Miles to return from patrol, when monitoring news feeds for super-incidents, when problem-solving aloud. This is oral self-soothing, well within normal adolescent range but pronounced enough to register as a tell: a hand to the chip bag is, for Ganke, what a hand to the cigarette pack would be for an earlier generation's worrier.

**Substances.** Caffeine: high and chronic, via soda and energy drinks; the energy-drink can is nearly a costume element. Alcohol: not depicted; age-appropriate absence. Nicotine: absent. Cannabis: absent. Other illicit substances: absent. He is, in the substance sense, a *clean* civilian — which, given the access his Spider-Man-adjacent social circle would theoretically provide, is itself a personality datum (he does not seek altered states; he prefers cognitive sharpness, which his preferred substances — caffeine and sugar — protect).

**Hydration.** Probably inadequate, by the dorm-snacker profile. Not clinical.

---

## 3. Activity, Cardiorespiratory, and Musculoskeletal Status

**Activity baseline.** Sedentary by clear preference. He is essentially never depicted running for exercise, in a gym, on a court, on a bike, or in any organized physical activity. The motor activities he does perform — walking to class, dorm-to-cafeteria transit, the occasional flight from a scene of acute danger when proximate to Miles's hero life — represent his entire cardiovascular load. Expected consequences: deconditioned aerobic capacity, low VO₂max relative to peers, mild muscular underdevelopment particularly in lower body and posterior chain, and the postural signature of the chronic-laptop adolescent (forward head, rounded shoulders, kyphotic upper back) that artists render almost reflexively when drawing him at rest.

**Fine motor.** Excellent and well-practiced. LEGO assembly, keyboard work, controller use, phone manipulation — all sustained, dexterous, fast. This is the one motor domain in which he is conspicuously skilled.

**Injuries from physical exertion.** None documented. He has not sprained, strained, fractured, or torn anything from his own movement, because he does not move enough to.

**Injuries from proximity to superhuman events.** Remarkably few given the years of exposure. Minor scrapes, bumps, and the occasional shaken-by-explosion-debris beat exist in the archive but rise to no significance — no concussion documented, no fractures, no lacerations requiring closure, no hospitalization. The protective bubble around him is partly Miles's own vigilance (Miles repeatedly extricates Ganke from danger zones, prioritizing him in triage), partly authorial. Either way, his nervous system has not been trained by repeated bodily emergencies into the kind of trauma-circuitry his hero-friend's body carries.

---

## 4. Surgical and Procedural History

**None documented.** No appendectomy, no tonsillectomy, no orthopedic intervention, no dental surgery foregrounded. By plausible inference: routine childhood vaccinations and pediatric visits; possible dental extractions; possibly some standard adolescent procedure, none of clinical narrative weight. The medical record is, in surgical terms, blank — which, again, is itself a fact: he has not had the formative experience of being put under, of waking up in a recovery room, of inhabiting the patient role. He has never been on the receiving end of a medical system's full attention.

---

## 5. Transformations, Exposures, and Enhancements

**None.** This is the most striking line of the file. Ganke has not been:

- Bitten by anything radioactive, genetically modified, or symbiotic.
- Exposed to OZ, Mutant Growth Hormone, the Terrigen Mists, Pym Particles, gamma radiation, cosmic radiation, the Power Cosmic, or any of the standard transformative agents accessible within the New York comics ecology.
- Bonded to a symbiote, granted a power ring, infused with a Nova Force, or otherwise vector for an exogenous abilities-package.
- Mind-controlled for plot-significant duration. Brief possession-or-influence beats may exist in event-tie-ins, but nothing has restructured his identity.
- Cloned, time-displaced into an alternate-future-self body, or aged/de-aged.
- Killed and resurrected.

The cumulative absence is the medical history's central feature. He occupies one of the most dangerous social positions in the Marvel street-level milieu and emerges, year after year, untransformed. The reading: he is one of the few characters in this corner of the universe whose **body is still his own**, in the strict sense that nothing supernatural has rewritten it. The psychological consequence is twofold. First, he has *no embodied trauma somatically encoded* — no flashback architecture, no scar-tissue triggers, no body-memory of violation. Second, he carries an *unearned-feeling safety* in a circle of friends who do not share it; he is the one whose body has not paid, and this likely contributes to the over-helpfulness, the eagerness to be useful in the only ways his unscarred body permits — informational, logistical, vocal.

---

## 6. The Pre-Incursion Discontinuity

A note that must appear in any honest somatic file: Ganke was, with most of his cohort, *physically rewritten* by the collapse of the Ultimate universe and the integration into the prime Marvel continuity during and after *Secret Wars* (2015). His body, in the strict cosmological sense, was reconstituted. He does not consciously carry the memory of this — Miles is the rare exception who retained dual-continuity awareness — and there is no on-panel indication that the transition produced somatic sequelae. But the file would be incomplete without noting that the subject's continuous body is, in fact, a continuity-edited body, and that any deep medical scan of him would, in principle, be scanning a re-instantiated form. This is meaningful chiefly as a frame: even the body assumed to be inviolate is, at the cosmic level, an authored object.

---

## 7. Psychiatric-Somatic Interface

The somatic costs of Ganke's actual life — chronic secret-keeping at developmentally formative stages, on-call status for emergencies he cannot resolve, vicarious exposure to violent outcomes against people he loves — should produce measurable physiological signatures. The expected panel would include: elevated resting heart rate variability indices of chronic sympathetic load, mild HPA-axis dysregulation, sleep fragmentation (already noted), and the somatized anxiety markers of chronic vigilance — bruxism, tension headaches, GI irregularity, weight drift.

The on-panel record shows: none of these explicitly. He does not complain of headaches, does not grip his jaw, does not retreat to the bathroom under stress, does not lose weight under acute story-arc pressure. The clinical reading must hold two possibilities simultaneously. Either (a) he is constitutionally resilient — a low-reactivity temperament that genuinely absorbs the load with minimal somatic cost, supported by his mature humor defense, his sublimation through tech and LEGO, and his secure attachment to Miles; or (b) the costs exist below the threshold of writerly attention, accruing as subclinical wear that has not yet been narratively explored. The honest position, given the years involved, is that *both* are true: he is genuinely resilient *and* the cost is genuinely there, banked, not yet drawn down.

The single behavioral symptom that *does* appear in the record — the disclosure leak, the chronic over-communicating, the secret that escapes him to Judge and then, in pattern, to others — should be understood medically as well as psychologically. It is, functionally, an *anxiety discharge with somatic relief*. Telling the secret lightens the load in a measurable phenomenological sense; he is regulating his own neuroendocrine state by redistributing the cognitive-affective burden. That this regulation strategy carries social cost is the central tragedy of his medical-psychological profile: his body is using a coping mechanism his ethics cannot endorse.

---

## 8. Healthcare Access and Use

By inference from his enrollment at a private gifted charter (Brooklyn Visions) and his presentation, he has continuous insurance access through family. There is no depicted ER visit, no depicted clinic visit, no depicted therapist. He has likely never sat in a mental-health professional's office. This is the single most consequential gap in his care: the one human in his life best positioned to benefit from an authorized confidant — someone with whom the secret could be fully discussed without ethical leakage — has no such confidant and has, by all evidence, not sought one. The role of secret-keeper to a superhero contains no provision for clinical containment, and Ganke's medical file is, in this sense, a file of *care not received* more than care delivered.

---

## 9. Summary of Somatic Risk Posture

He is, at present, a low-acute-risk, moderate-chronic-risk body. The acute profile is unremarkable: a healthy adolescent of sedentary habit, glasses-corrected vision, snack-heavy diet, adequate sleep when permitted, no substance liabilities, no surgical history, no transformation events. The chronic profile is the watch-list:

- **Metabolic drift.** The sedentary-plus-snack pattern, sustained into adulthood without correction, will produce the standard metabolic-syndrome trajectory in the third decade.
- **Postural-musculoskeletal degradation.** The laptop posture is already visible; the cervical and thoracic costs will accrue.
- **Sleep-circadian dysregulation.** Currently compensated; less compensable in adult contexts that impose fixed schedules.
- **Cumulative allostatic load** from chronic secret-keeping and vigilance, currently masked by adaptive defenses, with the disclosure-leak as the safety valve.
- **Absence of any care relationship** in which any of the above could be addressed.

The file closes on the observation it opened with: this is a body the world has not yet collected its debts from. The intactness is real, but the bill is accruing, and the subject has no account from which to pay it except the one labeled *the friendship* — and he has already, repeatedly, drawn on that.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: GANKE LEE

## Preamble

The body of the subject is, in surveillance terms, *low-yield and high-fidelity*: he produces few signals, but the signals he produces are extraordinarily stable across years of observation. He does not perform with his body; he leaks with it. What follows is the granular catalog — every documented and reasonably inferable bodily pattern across roughly a decade of continuous adolescent-to-late-adolescent observation, indexed by baseline and by state-shift (calm / acute stress / threat-proximal / intimacy).

---

## 1. Build, Frame, and Carriage

**Anthropometry.** Short for cohort (estimated 5'4"–5'6" through late adolescence, with limited longitudinal growth across the observation window). Soft-bodied: pronounced cheek-fat, rounded shoulders, low muscle definition, slight abdominal carriage. Hands small and short-fingered; nails kept short but unmanicured — bitten at the edges in periods of academic load, recovering to neutral during summer windows. Wrists narrow. Posture *kyphotic-default*: head forward of shoulders by approximately one to two centimeters past neutral, a screen-and-bed posture set deep into the musculoskeletal baseline.

**Carriage by state.**
- *Calm:* slouch deepens; weight distributed asymmetrically across one hip when standing, often with one arm braced on a hard surface (desk, doorframe, the back of Miles's chair).
- *Excited:* posture *paradoxically improves* — chest lifts, shoulders rotate back, head rises. The body recruits in service of the verbal stream. Notable: the only consistent moments he stands fully upright are when he is explaining something he loves.
- *Stressed:* shoulders rise toward the ears, neck shortens visibly, the kyphotic curl tightens by approximately five to eight degrees. Hands migrate to mid-torso and stay there.
- *Threat-proximal:* he *compacts*. Center of mass drops into the hips, knees soften, he becomes geometrically smaller and tends to position himself with a solid object (wall, furniture, Miles) between his torso and the threat vector. He does not freeze; he ducks.
- *Intimacy (with Bombshell / pursued romantic targets):* posture *destabilizes*. He becomes shorter, paradoxically — knees flex unconsciously, weight rocks heel-to-toe in a slow oscillation, hands occupy themselves with anything available (sleeves, the hem of a shirt, an object lifted and turned).

---

## 2. Gait and Locomotion

**Baseline gait.** Short stride, mild heel-strike, low cadence at rest, high cadence when summoned. Slight in-toeing on the right foot. No athletic carriage — the body has not been trained to move efficiently through space. He arrives places out of breath after stairs.

**Movement signatures.**
- The *snack-walk*: ambling, one hand occupied (bowl, bag, phone), pace dictated by whatever he is eating or reading.
- The *summoned-trot*: short, fast steps, arms held slightly bent at the elbows but not swinging — torso leads, legs catch up. Deployed when Miles calls or when a developing situation pulls him from horizontal.
- The *dorm-shuffle*: indoors, in socks, knees never fully extending. The signature ambulation of his natural habitat.

**Locomotion under threat.** Has demonstrated capacity for genuine running only under acute necessity. Form is poor — arms flap wide, head bobs, breath audibles within ten to fifteen meters. He gets where he is going; he does not enjoy it; he leans against the first available vertical surface upon arrival.

---

## 3. Facial Architecture and Expression

**Resting face.** Mouth slightly open at rest (an *adenoidal-pattern set* common in chronic mouth-breathers; whether structural or habitual is undetermined). Eyebrows neutral-high. Eyes behind glasses — wire-or-thin-plastic frames, consistently — that he pushes up the bridge of his nose with the index finger of whichever hand is free, approximately every ninety seconds when seated, more frequently when speaking.

**The glasses-push.** This is his single most reliable tic. The vector is bottom-up at the bridge, never lateral. Under stress the rate increases to roughly every twenty to thirty seconds and the contact lingers — the finger rests at the bridge for a full beat before withdrawing, sometimes followed by a brief pinch of the bridge with thumb and index. The pinch is a *stop-and-think* marker: he is buying processing time.

**Smile.** Wide, asymmetric (rises slightly higher on the left), exposes upper teeth and a thin band of upper gum. Genuine smile recruits the orbicularis oculi (Duchenne-positive); his social smile does not, and the difference is readable within two frames. He smiles by default during conversation — a *low-baseline-positive* face — which means the absence of the smile is itself the signal worth tracking.

**Brow and eye patterns.**
- *Curiosity:* eyebrows rise symmetrically; head tilts ten to fifteen degrees right.
- *Skepticism / "really?":* left eyebrow lifts alone; mouth corners pull asymmetrically down-left.
- *Worry:* the inner brow corners pull up and together (the classic distress configuration), held briefly, then deliberately released into a smile or quip. He *catches* worry on his face and removes it. This is one of the most consistent micro-patterns in the file: he does not let his face hold fear long enough to be witnessed.
- *Threat:* eyes widen, blink rate suppresses briefly (one to two seconds without blinking), then a hard double-blink resets him.

**Lip patterns.** Bites lower lip when concentrating on a screen. Presses lips together hard — a thin line — in the moments after he has said something he immediately regrets, especially in the disclosure-leak family of behaviors. Tongue periodically wets lower lip during sustained speech.

---

## 4. Hands, Fingers, and Object-Manipulation

The hands are the *primary tell-surface*. Where his face has been trained (largely by himself) to default-positive, his hands run uncensored.

**At rest with nothing to hold:** the hands seek each other. Default configuration is fingers laced loosely in lap or on desk; secondary configuration is one hand wrapped around the opposite wrist. Hands without an object are a state he finds mildly unbearable; the *time-to-acquisition* of a fidgetable object in any new environment is under thirty seconds.

**Fidget hierarchy** (in observed order of preference): a LEGO piece (any), a pen (clicked, never written with during fidgeting), his phone (flipped end-over-end in one hand), the corner of a hoodie sleeve (rolled between thumb and forefinger), the drawstring of the hoodie (chewed in private, twisted in company), the edge of whatever he is eating's packaging (folded into smaller and smaller squares).

**LEGO-specific motor sequences.** When building, the right hand sorts pieces by color and type into shallow piles arrayed in a semicircle in front of him; the left hand holds the in-progress assembly. He pre-stages the next three to five pieces in the order they will be installed — a small, durable expression of his cognitive style rendered as motor pattern. He builds with surprising speed and no measurable error rate. When *stress-building* (post-conflict, post-fright), the pre-staging shortens to one piece at a time and the build slows; the activity has shifted from construction to regulation.

**Typing posture.** Cross-legged on bed, laptop on knees or pillow, head tilted down, glasses sliding. Two-handed, fast, but mechanically untrained — he is a self-taught typist with idiosyncratic finger assignments. Wrists float; he has never been corrected. Keystroke cadence is bursty: long pauses for thought, then sustained runs.

**Phone handling.** Held in the right hand, thumb-scrolling, left hand cupping the right or occupied with food. Notifications produce a small chin-lift and eye-flick that is the only reflex faster than his glasses-push.

---

## 5. Verbal-Motor Patterning

Speech is one of his primary motor activities and merits anatomical-level cataloging.

**Cadence.** Fast, with frequent self-interruption. Mean words-per-minute well above adolescent norm. Sentences nest — he opens a clause, branches into a parenthetical, branches again, returns to original clause with a *"anyway"* or *"point being"* marker. The return-marker is reliable; he does not lose the thread.

**Filler inventory.** *"Like,"* *"so,"* *"okay but,"* *"I mean,"* *"the thing is,"* *"basically,"* *"dude."* The *"dude"* is reserved almost exclusively for Miles and rises in frequency under emotional weight — it functions as an attachment-vocative, a verbal hand on the shoulder.

**Reference-injection.** Approximately one in four sentences in extended speech contains a pop-culture or genre-template reference. Under stress this rises sharply — past one in two — and the references become more obscure, as if reaching deeper into the catalog for grip.

**Laughter.** Three distinct registers:
- A *short exhale-laugh* through the nose for low-grade amusement.
- A *full open-mouth laugh* with head tip back and one hand to the chest or stomach, reserved for genuine delight.
- A *high nervous laugh* — pitched up, brief, sustained for one beat too long — that appears in the half-second after he has said something he should not have. This is the most diagnostically valuable of the three; it is the leak-indicator.

**Speech under threat.** Cadence accelerates further. Volume *drops* — he becomes quieter under threat, not louder, which is operationally useful and worth noting. Sentence structure simplifies: he can produce short imperatives and information-dense fragments when the situation requires.

**Speech in intimacy.** Cadence *shatters*. He stammers, restarts, abandons sentences. The reference-injection vanishes — he loses his templates when genuinely exposed romantically, which is the only environment in which this happens.

---

## 6. Eating and Ingestion

**Frequency.** Near-constant low-grade ingestion across the waking day. Discrete meals are augmented by continuous grazing — cereal at unconventional hours, snack-bags on the desk, takeout containers archaeologically stratified in the dorm-room waste bin.

**Preferences.** Salt-dominant snacks (chips, crackers, pretzels); cereal eaten dry or with milk indifferently; takeout skews toward Korean-American and pan-Asian preferences with a heavy rotation through pizza and burgers as the default American adolescent baseline. No documented aversions. No depicted food-related anxieties.

**Mechanics.** Eats with mouth slightly open when speaking simultaneously (frequent). Chews quickly. Drinks soda or energy drinks from cans, not glasses; the can rests near the laptop, sweating onto whatever paper is adjacent. He does not use coasters.

**State-shifts.**
- *Stressed:* snacking accelerates; the *rate* of hand-to-mouth motion roughly doubles. The food is being used as a metronome more than as nutrition.
- *Acute crisis:* eating *stops entirely*. The reliable sign that something is genuinely wrong is the untouched snack.
- *Post-resolution:* eating *resumes with appetite increase* — a discharge meal, often shared, often verbally narrated as he eats.

**Hydration.** Underhydrated by clinical standards. Caffeinated beverages dominate; water is consumed reluctantly and usually at someone else's prompting.

---

## 7. Sleep Architecture

**Schedule.** Phase-delayed. Latency to sleep onset is long when the laptop is in bed with him (frequently the case). Bedtime drifts past midnight on weekdays, well past on weekends. Wake-time is school-enforced, producing a chronic mild sleep debt managed by weekend recovery sleep of nine to eleven hours.

**Position.** Sleeps curled, knees drawn partially up, on his side — most often the right side, facing the room rather than the wall, a not-incidental orientation given the frequency with which Miles enters and exits through the window. He has trained himself, whether deliberately or by adaptation, to sleep facing the entry point.

**Wake response.** Slow to consciousness from deep sleep; fast to consciousness when Miles enters the room. The differential is large and consistent — a *named-caller* arousal pattern indicating that some part of his sensory system remains tuned to a specific stimulus class even in sleep. Glasses are on the bedside surface within reach; the first motor sequence on waking is reach-and-don.

**Sleep talking / movement.** No documented parasomnia. He sleeps relatively still.

**Sleep-deprivation presentation.** Glasses are pushed up the bridge more frequently. Speech-cadence slows by a measurable margin. The reference-injection rate drops — fatigue thins the catalog. Snacking increases. The high nervous laugh appears at lower thresholds, meaning his disclosure-risk is highest when he is tired.

---

## 8. Grooming and Self-Presentation

**Hair.** Black, straight, kept at a medium-short cut with minimal styling. He runs a hand through it absently when thinking; the gesture is left-handed and starts at the temple. Under sustained stress the hand-through-hair gesture becomes a *grab-and-hold* — fingers close on a tuft, brief tug, release. This is his closest analog to a self-harm gesture and remains well within normative adolescent range.

**Skin.** Adolescent acne typical of cohort, primarily forehead and chin, manages with inconsistent washing. No picking observed beyond age-typical.

**Wardrobe baseline.** Layered: a t-shirt (graphic-printed: bands, games, comics, the occasional ironic slogan) under an unzipped hoodie, jeans or sweats, sneakers worn past their structural integrity. The hoodie is the constant; he owns several but cycles them in a clearly favored order. He does not dress for weather; he dresses for the indoor temperature he expects.

**Wardrobe under intimacy-stakes.** Notable deviation: when meeting Bombshell or in romantic-adjacent contexts, the layer-stack tightens. He swaps the hoodie for an actual jacket; the graphic tee is replaced with something monochrome; the sneakers get tied properly. The grooming uptick is small but real, and is the most reliable behavioral indicator of his romantic investment level.

**Scent.** Body spray applied unevenly, occasionally over-applied — the standard adolescent over-correction. Glasses are wiped on the hem of his shirt with a circular motion of the thumb; lens cleanliness is poor.

---

## 9. Spatial and Proxemic Patterns

**Personal habitat.** His half of the dorm is denser than Miles's: more objects, more visible projects, more food. The LEGO sets are displayed; the laptop is the centerpiece. He occupies the bed as a primary workstation rather than a sleep surface — bed, pillow propped against wall, knees up, laptop balanced. The desk is for staging.

**Routes.** Predictable. Dorm → cafeteria → classroom → dorm, with the cafeteria visit timed to avoid peak crowding. He has memorized the BVA stairwells and prefers a specific one (the less-trafficked east-side staircase, inferred from his consistent appearance from that direction in dorm-corridor scenes). Off-campus, he moves between dorm, library, and a small rotation of food establishments within walking radius. He does not travel solo by subway with comfort.

**Interpersonal proxemics.** With Miles: very close, frequently touching at low intensity (shoulder-bumps, leaning on each other on shared furniture, hands passing objects without visual confirmation — a high-trust signature). With acquaintances: standard cohort distance. With authority figures: a half-step further back than peers, body slightly angled rather than fronted. With Bombshell: oscillating — he closes distance, panics, retreats a half-step, recovers, closes again. The proxemic dance is visible to any observer.

**Touch tolerance.** Receives touch easily from Miles and from family-frame figures. Initiates touch sparingly. Does not embrace fully — his hugs are one-armed and brief, with a back-pat termination. The exception, again, is Miles, with whom he has been observed in genuine two-armed contact during emotional peaks.

---

## 10. Sexual and Romantic Somatics

The record is thin by design — he is a depicted adolescent and the canon does not document sexual behavior. What is documentable is the *somatic prelude*: the body's behavior in proximity to desire.

**Arousal-proximal pattern.** Flushing across the cheeks and ears (the ears redden first and are visible past his hairline). Vocal-cord constriction producing a slight pitch-rise. Increased glasses-push rate. Hands fully occupied with anything available. The smile shifts to a *contained* smile — corners up, lips pressed together — that is qualitatively different from his social grin.

**Approach behavior.** Indirect. He orbits, makes contact at the verbal level first, escalates physical proximity only on clear invitation. Has not demonstrated the capacity to initiate physical romantic contact without prior reciprocation cue. His romantic confidence is *receptive*, not *projective*.

**Rejection / setback response.** Verbal recovery is fast (a joke, a self-deprecation); somatic recovery is slow. Posture flattens for hours afterward; snacking increases; the laptop is opened to a comfort-content rotation.

---

## 11. State-Shift Summary Matrix

A compressed table of the most diagnostically valuable shifts:

| Signal | Calm | Stressed | Threat-Proximal | Intimacy |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Posture | Slouched, asymmetric | Curled tighter | Compacted, ducking | Destabilized, rocking |
| Glasses-push rate | ~90 sec | ~20–30 sec | Suppressed (frozen) | Elevated, lingering |
| Speech rate | Fast | Faster | Faster but quieter | Stammered, restarted |
| Reference-injection | 1 in 4 | 1 in 2 | Drops to short imperatives | Vanishes |
| Snacking | Continuous low | Doubled | Stops | Erratic |
| Smile | Default-positive | Forced, gum-line | Suppressed, lips thin | Contained, closed-lip |
| Hands | Object-seeking | Hair, sleeve, drawstring | Mid-torso, still | Anything available |
| Voice volume | Moderate | Moderate-loud | *Drops* | Drops |
| Nervous laugh | Absent | Occasional | Absent | Frequent |

---

## 12. The One Signal That Matters Most

If the file is to flag a single bodily signature as the operationally critical one, it is this: **the high nervous laugh, one beat too long, followed by lips pressed thin and an immediate glasses-push.** This is the post-disclosure micro-sequence. It is the body's confession that the mouth has just made one. Every documented instance of subject leaking a secret he was asked to hold has been preceded or immediately followed by this three-part somatic chord. It is the most reliable predictor of compromised information in the entire file, and the surveillance-grade reason it is named here is that the subject himself does not appear to know he is doing it.

That is the body of Ganke Lee: small, soft, verbal, gestural, transparent in exactly the place he most needs opacity, and otherwise the most steady-state organism in the entire perimeter around Miles Morales.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — GANKE LEE
## Section: Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 1. Attachment Classification — Primary Read

Subject presents as **secure-base attached with a thin anxious overlay specific to information-management.** This is an unusual configuration and requires precision: most secure individuals do not have a dedicated anxiety vector. Ganke does, and it has a clear etiology — he became, in early adolescence, the sole custodian of a piece of information whose disclosure would catastrophically reshape the life of his most loved person. The anxiety is not constitutional; it is **load-induced**, narrowly scoped, and behaviorally legible only along the disclosure axis. Across every other relational dimension — proximity tolerance, separation, repair, conflict, novelty — he scores in the secure range.

The secure baseline is observable in dozens of micro-behaviors across the publication record:

- He does not check whether Miles will come back; he assumes return and orients himself toward what he'll do when Miles arrives (laptop open, snack acquired, briefing prepared). Anxious-attached subjects produce reassurance-seeking on separation; Ganke produces **task continuity**.
- He tolerates being lied to about Miles's whereabouts in early issues (before disclosure) without escalation — confusion, mild concern, no abandonment-panic signature.
- He repairs ruptures without keeping score. After the Judge-disclosure confrontation in *Ultimate Comics: Spider-Man* (2011) #9–10, he does not litigate his motives or demand acknowledgment of his good intentions; he absorbs the rebuke and adjusts. No residue carries into subsequent issues.
- He does not protest-test the bond. He never pulls away to see whether Miles will come find him. This is among the most diagnostic absences in his record.

### 2. Origins — Inferred Developmental Architecture

The Lee household is barely depicted on panel, which is itself information; the subject does not narrate his family of origin into his social space, and writers have not built that bench. From the negative-space evidence we can construct a probable origin pattern:

- **Parental investment was high enough to produce a securely attached child.** Brooklyn Visions Academy is a competitive boarding charter; placement there is the product of years of parental scaffolding (test prep, paperwork, financial commitment or scholarship pursuit). The child arrived at BVA already academically oriented, socially fluent, and able to room with a stranger without separation distress. These are downstream markers of a competent caregiving environment.
- **Parental presence was high enough to model verbal warmth and humor, but emotionally narrow enough to teach him not to bring his weather inside.** His near-total reticence about his own internal states, paired with his absolute fluency in tracking others', is the signature of a child raised in a household where *being fine* was the price of being well-loved — not punitively, but ambiently. Korean-American second-generation households frequently transact love through provision and achievement rather than through verbal emotional excavation; this is not pathology, it is a culturally specific affective grammar, and it leaves the subject with the precise asymmetry he displays: deeply available to others, structurally unpracticed at requesting availability for himself.
- **Sibling position is undetermined on the published record**, but his caretaker-style deflection and his comfort in a supporting orbit are weakly consistent with either an older-sibling-of-a-needier-younger or an only-child-with-high-adult-exposure profile. He reads adults fluently — see his interactions with Jefferson and Rio Morales, BVA faculty, and later Aaron Davis — at a level that suggests he spent meaningful early time among them rather than predominantly among peers.

The childhood produced a child who **trusts the world to hold him** (the secure foundation) but who **does not expect the world to ask after him** (the caretaker overlay). He learned that he is safe and that he is responsible for the comfort of others. He did not learn that anyone is responsible for his.

### 3. The Bonding Protocol

Ganke bonds **fast, verbal, and through shared cognitive frame.** The activation sequence is consistent across every depicted relationship:

1. **Reference-deployment.** He throws out a piece of pop-culture, technical, or genre material as a probe. If the other person catches it, he extends the riff; if they don't, he translates and re-throws at a lower threshold.
2. **Service-offer.** Within hours of registering interest in another person, he offers something useful — information, a build, an introduction, an alibi. Service is his love-language and his calling card.
3. **Inside-joke installation.** He coins or reinforces a private vocabulary with the new bond — nicknames, callbacks, repeated bits. This converts the relationship from generic to specific quickly, and it functions as a *portable* bond marker he can deploy to reactivate intimacy across time.
4. **Physical proximity without physical contact.** He occupies the same room, same couch, same orbit, for long unstructured durations. He does not touch much. The bond is established by *parallel presence* — both on laptops, both eating, both half-watching something — rather than by ritualized contact.

The protocol is efficient. Most of his significant bonds — Miles, Judge, Bombshell, Barbara-as-acquaintance, peripheral BVA classmates — were operational within a single shared scene of meaningful duration.

### 4. The Master Template — Miles Morales

The relationship with Miles is the **template against which every other relational behavior should be read.** The shape of it:

- **Asymmetry, voluntary and stable.** Ganke knows more about Miles's life than Miles knows about Ganke's, and this is by Ganke's design, not Miles's neglect. When Miles asks (which he does, periodically, in moments of conscience throughout the Bendis and Ahmed runs), Ganke deflects with a joke and redirects to Miles's problem. The asymmetry is *maintained* by the supposedly disadvantaged party.
- **Loyalty without possessiveness.** When Miles forms new primary bonds — Katie Bishop in the Ultimate run, Barbara Rodriguez in the Ahmed run, the broader hero peer group in *Champions* — Ganke does not retract, sulk, or compete. He *integrates*. He learns the new person, slots himself into the expanded constellation, and continues offering the same services without contraction. This is rare; most adolescent best-friend dynamics include at least one observable jealousy episode. Ganke's record contains none.
- **The disclosure leak as the only durable conflict node.** Every significant rupture between Ganke and Miles traces to the same behavior: Ganke metabolizing the burden of Miles's secret by sharing it, slightly, with one more person. The leak to Judge is the prototype; the diffusion of awareness across the *Spider-Man* (2016) peer group is the chronic version. Miles experiences this as betrayal; Ganke experiences it as load management. **Both readings are accurate.** This is the only domain in which Ganke is not fully reliable to Miles, and it is the precise domain where Ganke's own unmet needs deform his otherwise impeccable care.
- **Repair velocity is exceptional.** Ruptures resolve within an issue, usually within a scene. Ganke does not negotiate apology terms; he absorbs the rebuke, signals understanding, and returns to function. This is secure-attachment repair — the bond is assumed to survive, and the work is restoration, not adjudication.

The template, distilled: **proximity without demand; service without ledger; loyalty without possession; one calibrated failure mode in the precise place where the loved person's needs collide with his own unspoken ones.**

### 5. The Disclosure Leak — Deep Reading

This deserves separate treatment because it recurs across every era and is the single repeatable relational failure in the file.

The leak is not malicious, not careless in the trivial sense, and not the product of poor impulse control in general (he sustains long technical tasks, completes academic work, manages multiple competing demands). It is **domain-specific impulse-bleed under chronic affective load.** The mechanism:

- He is given a secret that exceeds his developmental capacity to hold alone (he is 13–14 at the original Ultimate-run disclosure).
- He has no authorized confidant — Miles is the subject of the secret, his parents are unsafe recipients by definition, school authorities are out of bounds, no therapist is in the picture.
- The pressure accumulates. His regulatory defenses (humor, LEGO, snacking, sleep displacement) handle the steady-state load but degrade under acute spikes — a near-death of Miles, a close call with the parents, a new villain appearance.
- At the degradation threshold, the system discharges by **distributing the secret to one trusted other.** Judge first; later, by a similar mechanism, the diffusion to peers in the 2016 run.
- After discharge, baseline returns, defenses resume function, until the next spike.

This is **functionally an affect-regulation behavior wearing the costume of a security breach.** Miles experiences only the breach; Ganke is not articulate enough about his own interior to name the regulation. Neither party has the conceptual vocabulary to address what is actually happening, and so it recurs.

The structural fact is that Miles, by giving Ganke the secret, conscripted him into a job for which he was developmentally undermanned and provided him no support infrastructure for. The leak is the predictable consequence. The remarkable thing is not that Ganke leaks; it is that he leaks so little, so slowly, and to people who turn out, mostly, to be manageable inclusions.

### 6. Distrust, Betrayal, Repair

**Distrust** in Ganke does not present as suspicion. It presents as **silent withdrawal of the inside-joke layer.** When he stops referencing private material with someone, when he stops offering service unsolicited, when he goes to parallel-presence-without-verbal-bid — the bond is being downgraded. This has been depicted only rarely (his cooling toward characters who threaten Miles, his wary handling of certain adults in the Ahmed run) but the signature is consistent.

**Betrayal by others** he absorbs with disproportionate equanimity. When peers fail him — and they do, episodically — he does not catalogue. The grievance does not surface as later weapon. Two readings: (a) he has internalized that his own grievances are lower-priority than the bond's continuance; (b) he genuinely does not experience these as betrayals because his expectations of others are calibrated low enough to be rarely violated. The two readings are not mutually exclusive and probably co-exist.

**Betrayal by himself** — the leak — he processes with shame but not catastrophe. He does not spiral, does not perform contrition theatrically, does not punish himself visibly. He apologizes once, well, and adjusts behavior in the short term. The fact that the behavior recurs suggests the adjustment is situational rather than structural — he has not solved the underlying regulation problem, only the immediate instance.

**Repair** he initiates faster than the wounded party expects. His first move post-rupture is almost always a service-bid (offering tech help, information, a meal procurement) rather than a verbal apology. The bid is the apology. This is consistent with his caretaker training: *do, don't say.*

### 7. Intimacy and Dependency

**Intimacy with Ganke runs wide and shallow on his side, deep and narrow on others'.** People feel close to him quickly because his attention is genuine and his warmth is uncostly. They are often surprised, later, to realize how little they know about him. He is intimate in the giving direction and reserved in the receiving direction, and the asymmetry is rarely noticed because his deflections are warm.

**Dependency** patterns:
- He **allows others to depend on him without resentment.** Miles depends on him for alibis, comms, emotional grounding, baseline social anchoring at BVA. Ganke meets these demands as a matter of course.
- He **does not visibly depend on others.** Not because he doesn't need anything — he obviously does — but because his asks are encoded as jokes ("you owe me food"), as service-bids he expects reciprocally without naming the reciprocity, or as adjacencies (sitting near someone rather than requesting their attention).
- He has **one secret dependency he has never named:** the need for someone who can hold the cost of his role. He has never had this. The Bombshell pursuit may have been, in part, an unconscious search for it — a partner adjacent enough to the hero-world to absorb the burden — though the relationship as written has not developed that capacity.

### 8. Romantic Pattern (Bombshell and the Broader Signature)

His romantic mode is **anxious-eager, ill-defended, and structurally counter-conformist.** In a life otherwise organized around rule-following and risk-minimization, his single domain of demonstrated risk-tolerance is the choice of love-object. Lana Baumgartner is criminal-adjacent, socially marked, and outside the BVA respectability frame. He pursues her openly, fumblingly, without strategy.

Read against his caretaker profile, this is coherent: **romance is the one domain in which he asks to be seen for himself, separate from his function in Miles's life.** He cannot ask Miles for that without disrupting the template; he cannot ask his parents for it without breaking the household grammar; he can ask a romantic partner for it because the role permits the request. The risk-tolerance is the measure of the unmet need.

He is, in pursuit, the **least defended version of himself** that the record shows. The jokes thin out. The deflections fail. His ordinary smoothness becomes visible as a smoothness, because in courtship it stops working. This is also, not incidentally, the only context in which his published affect range expands beyond the cool baseline — embarrassment, hope, mild despair, recover, repeat.

### 9. Relationship to Authority

He **manages adults skillfully and without ideological resistance.** Teachers, parents (Miles's, by extension), administrators, later Aaron Davis — he reads them, deploys appropriate register, complies where compliance is cheap and dissimulates where it is not. He is neither rebel nor toady; he is a **competent under-the-radar operator**, and authority figures generally like him because he gives them no reason not to.

This is template-consistent: he does not require the validation of authority because his self-concept does not depend on hierarchy. He requires only the continuance of the bonds he has chosen, and those bonds are peer-bonds. Authority is environment, not source.

### 10. Relationship to the Hero-Adjacent Peer Group

As the constellation around Miles expanded across the runs — Bombshell, Goldballs, Fabio, Starling, Shift, Billie, and the floating cast of BVA students who came into proximity with the secret — Ganke developed a **second-tier role as the social interpreter and de facto switchboard.** He knows who knows what, who can be trusted with which fragment, who needs which kind of handling. He is the only civilian in the network with full strategic awareness of the network's composition.

He performs this role without seeking credit for it, which means most members of the peer group underestimate his centrality. They experience him as Miles's roommate and the funny one. They do not generally register that he is **the human protocol layer** keeping the social architecture of Miles's double life functional.

### 11. The Template, Compressed

Across every relationship — Miles, Judge, Bombshell, parents, faculty, the expanded peer group — the same shape recurs:

> **Approach fast and warm. Install a private register. Offer service before being asked. Maintain proximity without demand. Carry the other person's interior while concealing his own. Tolerate asymmetry without protest. Repair via service-bid, not verbal accounting. Discharge accumulated affective load by leaking, narrowly, the thing he was asked to hold. Return to baseline. Resume.**

It is a **caretaker template grafted onto a secure base.** It works extraordinarily well for the people he loves and exacts a quiet, unbilled cost from him that has not yet, in the publication record, come due. The relational future of the subject — the part of his file not yet written — turns on whether anyone in his life develops the capacity to *reverse the asymmetry* and ask after him with the same patience he has spent on them. No one currently in his orbit has shown that capacity. The latent question of his attachment architecture is whether he will, before the load exceeds his defenses, find someone who can.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — GANKE LEE
## SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

### Preface: Why this section is the spine of the file

Every other section in this dossier — medical, psychiatric, personality, relational — terminates here. Ganke Lee has been carrying, since approximately age thirteen, an information load whose accidental discharge would (a) reveal Spider-Man's civilian identity, (b) destroy the Morales family's domestic security, (c) compromise his own physical safety against actors who routinely murder leverage-relations of costumed targets, and (d) end the central friendship of his life. He has carried this load for years across two cosmological continuities without clinical decompensation. That is not luck. That is *architecture* — a stable, internally coherent stack of psychological defenses, most of them mature, a few of them subclinically problematic, organized around a central operational metaphor (assembly, modularity, the LEGO model of self) that he applies, largely without awareness, to the management of his own interior.

The defensive stack is presented below ranked from most primitive (least adaptive, ego-fragmenting) to most mature (Vaillant tier IV — humor, sublimation, altruism, suppression, anticipation). The notable finding of this section is the *shape* of the stack: Ganke's lower tiers are nearly empty. He does not splitting, does not project, does not somatize, does not act out. His architecture is unusually clean for an adolescent under chronic stress. The risk in the architecture is not what is in it; the risk is what isn't — specifically, the absence of any *vertical* discharge route. He has no upward channel to an authorized adult, no peer of equal burden, no therapist, no journal, no faith practice. The architecture is robust laterally and fragile vertically. Pressure that cannot be metabolized horizontally accumulates and discharges through the one defective valve in the system: information dispersal.

---

### TIER I — PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Psychotic / Narcissistic)

**Largely absent. Their absence is itself the headline.**

- **Splitting:** Not observed. Ganke retains nuanced, integrated representations even of figures who have wronged him or Miles. He continues to like Judge after the betrayal pivot in *USM* (2011) #6–10 rather than recategorizing him as enemy. He treats Bombshell's villain past as a fact to be integrated, not a binary to be resolved. He has never demonstrated the all-good/all-bad collapse characteristic of borderline organization.
- **Projective identification:** Not observed. He does not induce his own affect states in Miles and then experience them as coming back; the affect traffic in their friendship runs the other direction (Miles's intensities are absorbed by Ganke, processed, returned diluted).
- **Denial (psychotic-grade):** Not observed. He accepts unwelcome facts on first presentation — including, critically, the fact of the spider-bite and the powers (*USM* 2011 #2), which most adolescents would reject reflexively before integrating. His reality-testing under extraordinary input is exceptional.
- **Distortion / delusional projection:** Not observed.

The clean Tier I is diagnostically meaningful: it rules out the primitive personality organizations and establishes that whatever vulnerabilities Ganke has are organized at a higher developmental level.

---

### TIER II — IMMATURE DEFENSES (Borderline / Adolescent-Typical)

**Sparse. One operative mechanism of consequence.**

- **Acting out:** Not observed in conventional form (no impulsive destructive behavior, no rule-breaking for discharge). The one near-equivalent — leaking the secret to Judge — does not fit acting-out structure because it is *cognitive* and *prosocial* in intent rather than impulsive and aggressive.
- **Passive aggression:** Notably absent. This deserves its own paragraph because it is the *expected* defense for his structural position. The best-friend-of-the-hero archetype, in adolescent psychology and in genre fiction alike, routinely develops passive-aggressive expressions of being-eclipsed: lateness, sulks, gossip, micro-sabotage, weaponized helplessness. None of this is in the record. Across writers — Bendis, Ahmed, Ziglar — Ganke has not once been depicted withholding, sulking, or undermining. The absence is so durable it must be read as structural, not coincidental.
- **Fantasy (schizoid escape):** Mildly present but channelized into constructive forms. He does *use* fantasy (LEGO, pop-culture, genre templates) but he does not retreat into it as substitute for relationship. His fantasy is generative and shared, not regressive and solitary.
- **Hypochondriasis:** Not observed.
- **Idealization (immature form):** Mild. He idealizes Miles's heroism somewhat, which is age- and role-appropriate; it does not impair his reality-testing about Miles's limits.

**The one operative Tier II mechanism: somatic discharge via consumption.** Ganke's near-continuous on-panel eating, snacking, and energy-drink intake is a low-grade oral-incorporation defense — affect regulation through ingestion. It does not rise to disordered eating, but it is the most primitive defense reliably active in his system. Under stress he chews. The body is being managed through the mouth and the screen rather than the breath or the muscle. This is consistent with sedentary-coded adolescents in high-affect environments and is unremarkable in isolation; in the context of his total stress load, it is one of the few signs that the load is being absorbed somewhere.

---

### TIER III — NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Intermediate, Workably Adaptive)

**This is where most of Ganke's working defensive labor occurs.** The bulk of his daily regulation runs on Tier III mechanisms — adaptive enough to function, inflexible enough to occasionally fail in characteristic ways.

#### 1. Intellectualization (primary neurotic defense)

Ganke metabolizes emotionally loaded material by converting it into informational, technical, or analytical content. When Miles is in danger, Ganke responds with *plans*, with *data*, with *scenarios* — the cognitive frame keeps the affect at distance. When the spider-bite reveal occurs, his first move is *curiosity-as-triage*: what can you do, how does it work, can you do it again. He converted what should have been a traumatic disclosure into a research problem inside one conversation. This is the same defense Vaillant catalogued in successful Harvard cohort subjects under wartime and bereavement stress — it works, and it works most of Ganke's life, with one cost: it makes his own affect occasionally illegible to himself. He knows what he *thinks* about things. He is less reliably current on what he *feels* about them.

#### 2. Rationalization

Closely paired with intellectualization. The Judge disclosure is the textbook case: he tells Judge and produces, in real time, a rational account of why this is *helpful* (backup, mutual aid, distributed risk), which displaces the actual driver (the load of the secret was producing distress and needed somewhere to go). The rationalization is sincere — he is not lying to Miles or to himself; he genuinely believes the justification at the moment of production. This is the signature of rationalization rather than deception: the post-hoc reason feels like the real reason to the agent.

#### 3. Displacement

Operates onto inanimate objects, primarily LEGO and code. Frustration, anxiety, and unspent agitation get worked out on bricks, builds, debugging, configuration. He does not displace onto people — he does not snap at Miles, snipe at parents, scapegoat teachers. The displacement targets are consistently objects, which is one of the cleanest possible directions for this defense to take.

#### 4. Reaction formation (mild)

Faint. He occasionally performs a slightly larger version of *unbothered* than he actually is — particularly around Miles's expanding hero-social circle, where the appropriate adolescent response would be at least a flicker of displacement-anxiety and what is shown instead is uniform, slightly emphatic, support. The emphasis is the tell. He is not *faking* support; he is over-producing it slightly to seal off the small envy he would otherwise have to acknowledge. This is reaction formation in its low-grade neurotic form and it is functional.

#### 5. Isolation of affect

The mechanism most responsible for the narrow on-panel emotional range noted in the Psychological section. Ganke can describe extraordinarily high-stakes events (his best friend nearly died last night; he himself was nearly collateral) without the corresponding affect. The content is reported; the feeling is sequestered. This is not flatness or alexithymia — when the affect is summoned (Bombshell scenes, certain Miles-distress scenes) it is present and appropriate — but the *default* setting separates content from feeling. This is what permits him to keep functioning through the chronic stress load. It is also what makes his eventual decompensation, if it comes, likely to be sudden rather than gradual: isolation-of-affect defenses tend to hold until they break rather than fray.

#### 6. Undoing

Minor. After leaks and disclosures he undertakes compensatory loyalty performances — extra help, extra availability, the small reparative gestures that follow rupture. These are sincere repair behaviors but also carry the trace structure of undoing: the wrong-act is symbolically reversed through a counter-act of equivalent visibility.

#### 7. Repression

Operative around his own desires and ambitions. Ganke's interior — what he wants for himself, what he fears for himself, what he envies, what he mourns — is consistently under-articulated. The repression is selective: information about *others* is fluent and accessible; information about *self* is throttled. This is the *caretaker repression* common in friends-of-the-extraordinary, in younger siblings of high-need siblings, in children of high-affect parents. He has organized his attention outward as a stable structural choice and the inward channel has atrophied at the same rate.

---

### TIER IV — MATURE DEFENSES (Vaillant's Adaptive)

**This is where Ganke is genuinely strong — strong enough that the strength itself becomes part of the risk profile, because it masks how much labor the lower tiers are doing.**

#### 1. Humor (his signature defense)

Vaillant defines mature humor as the capacity to bear painful affect by representing it in a form that produces pleasure without distorting the affect's content. Ganke meets this definition with unusual purity. He does not joke *instead of* feeling; he jokes *while* feeling, and the joke preserves the truth of the situation rather than erasing it. The recurring pattern — joke first, competent action second — is not avoidance; it is *announcement* of presence followed by deployment of capacity. The joke says *I am here and conscious and the situation has not seized me*; the action follows. This is among the highest-functioning defenses in the human repertoire and it is the load-bearing element of his entire architecture. The dossier's title-phrase for him — *load-bearing humor* — is psychologically literal.

**Risk note:** the defense is so reliable that he has not been required to develop alternates. If the situation arises that humor cannot reach — Miles dead, his own family in crisis, a betrayal he caused that he cannot joke past — he has no equivalently mature backup. Mature defenses tend to be domain-specific; humor reaches most domains but not all.

#### 2. Sublimation

The LEGO obsession, the coding, the technical fabrications for Miles's alibis, the constructive engagement with information systems — all are sublimations of high-arousal energy into productive, socially valued, satisfying activity. The LEGO motif is the cleanest case: under stress he builds. The construction binds anxious arousal into a coherent object whose completion provides closure. The neurobiological account (focused attention, predictable reward, motor-cognitive integration) and the psychoanalytic account (binding of drive-energy in symbolic activity) both describe the same observable behavior. This is sublimation in the textbook form and it has carried him through years of conditions that would have produced symptom formation in a less defended adolescent.

#### 3. Affiliation

His default coping strategy is *be with*. Stress produces calls, group chats, presence, proximity. He does not isolate under load; he gathers. This is a mature defense and a protective one — affiliation under stress is among the strongest predictors of long-term resilience in longitudinal studies. The risk in his particular case is that his primary affiliation target (Miles) is often *unavailable* due to hero-duty, and his affiliation toolkit does not extend smoothly to substitute targets. He gathers around Miles; when Miles is absent, the gathering instinct is denied its object and runs unsatisfied.

#### 4. Altruism

His help to Miles is genuinely altruistic in the Vaillant sense — pleasure taken in service-to-other that is not reducible to expected reciprocity or self-aggrandizement. He does not keep ledger. He does not extract gratitude. He does not weaponize favors. The help is the reward.

#### 5. Suppression (conscious)

He demonstrably can hold things he chooses to hold. The secret has, in most circumstances, been held — the leaks are the exception, not the rule. He can park anxiety, defer reactions, table conversations to better times. Suppression is the cleanest of the mature defenses and is reliably available to him.

#### 6. Anticipation

Strongest in technical/operational domains: he prepares, scouts, plans, builds redundancy into Miles's cover stories, fabricates contingencies. Weaker in personal/emotional domains: he does not anticipate his own future affective states well, does not plan for his own emotional needs, does not prepare himself for foreseeable losses (Miles graduating, Miles moving on, Miles being injured).

---

### COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (Distinct from Defenses)

Defenses regulate affect; compensations construct *role* and *value*. Ganke's compensations are visible enough to map.

#### 1. Niche construction — the irreplaceability strategy

He has, semi-consciously, built a niche in Miles's life that is structurally his alone: the *only* civilian who knows everything, the *only* technical operator at hand, the *only* friend predating the hero-identity. This niche cannot be filled by a girlfriend, a fellow hero, a mentor, or a parent — they are all categorically other roles. The niche makes him secure without requiring he be exceptional in any larger field. This is a sophisticated and ultimately healthy compensation: he has solved the *how do I matter to this person whose life is now extraordinary* problem by being the one thing the extraordinary cannot supply for itself — continuity.

#### 2. Knowledge as currency

His pop-culture, technical, and genre knowledge is currency he reliably has when other forms of capital (athleticism, heroism, beauty, glamour) he does not. He has invested heavily in this currency because the return on it, in his particular social ecology, is high. This is healthy compensation — playing to genuine strength — rather than overcompensation, because the strength is real.

#### 3. The support-role preference

The genuine preference for the support role rather than the spotlight is one of his rarest features. Most adolescents adjacent to extraordinary peers develop spotlight-envy as a near-universal subroutine; he has not. The preference functions compensatorily — it converts what would otherwise be a chronic dissatisfaction (being not-the-hero) into a chronic satisfaction (being exactly where he wants to be). Whether the preference is bedrock or itself a higher-order defense (a sophisticated reaction formation against unbearable envy) is the single most interesting unresolved question in his profile. The record does not yet decide it. The behavioral evidence is consistent either way.

#### 4. The LEGO operational code

Beyond sublimation, the LEGO practice serves as a *cognitive operating system* he applies analogically across domains: relationships as builds, problems as assembly, identity as modular construction permitting iteration and repair. This is a compensatory worldview — it gives him a stable epistemology in a life adjacent to a friend whose epistemology is permanently destabilized by superhuman events. He has chosen a frame in which the world is *constructible*, and the choice protects him from the existential vertigo his proximity to costumed reality would otherwise produce.

#### 5. Romantic pursuit as self-individuation

The Bombshell pursuit is compensatory in a specific direction: it is the one domain in which he is pursuing being *chosen for himself*, separate from his function in Miles's narrative. The pursuit's anxious-eager quality reflects how *exposed* he is in this domain — the rest of his life has thick defensive padding, and the romantic domain is where he steps out from behind the architecture and asks to be seen.

---

### THE DEFECTIVE VALVE — Information Dispersal

The one mechanism in the architecture that consistently fails in the same direction. It does not belong cleanly to any Vaillant tier because it is a *discharge route* rather than a defense proper — but it is the route through which un-metabolized burden exits the system when the other defenses are at capacity.

Mechanism: under chronic load with no authorized confidant, the pressure of held information seeks lateral discharge to trusted peers. The discharge is rationalized in real time as *helpful* (Judge as backup, later disclosures as practical necessity). The discharge briefly reduces the load and is briefly relieving. The cost is borne by Miles, whose secret's perimeter expands without his consent.

This is the architectural vulnerability. Every other defense in the stack is oriented inward (regulate Ganke's own affect) or sideways (help Miles); the defective valve is the only mechanism that *transfers cost* to the protected other. It is also the only mechanism Ganke does not appear to have insight into. He has not, on record, recognized the leak pattern as a pattern. He treats each instance as a separate practical judgment. Until he can name the pattern, he cannot defend against it.

---

### What the Stack Predicts

A defensive architecture this clean at Tier I, this sparse at Tier II, this loaded at Tier III–IV, with a single recurrent low-tier leak — predicts the following trajectory absent intervention:

1. **Continued high-functioning performance** through late adolescence and early adulthood. The mature defenses will carry him.
2. **Periodic disclosure-incidents** at intervals roughly correlated with stress-load peaks (academic crises, romantic ruptures, Miles-injury events). Each will be rationalized; none will be recognized as recurrence.
3. **Slow accumulation of repressed self-content** — desires, ambitions, griefs about his own life — that no current channel is metabolizing. This will eventually require either a relationship that opens the inward channel (a partner, a therapist, an unexpected confidant) or symptom formation.
4. **A late, possibly singular, decompensation event** if humor and sublimation are simultaneously denied access to a sufficiently large affect — most likely a serious harm to Miles. Because his mature defenses have never been comprehensively defeated, he has no rehearsed protocol for their failure.

The architecture's headline finding: Ganke Lee is one of the more psychologically intact adolescents in his social ecology, and the single greatest threat to that intactness is that no one — including Ganke — has yet noticed how much weight the architecture is actually holding.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE: GANKE LEE

## Preliminary Note on Method and Timescale

A standard longitudinal profile assumes decades of observable life. Ganke Lee's publication history (2011–present) provides roughly a decade of in-text observation, but the *in-universe* developmental window is narrower still — sliding-time compression has held him between approximately ages thirteen and seventeen across that decade. The honest longitudinal frame is therefore **developmental-phase** rather than calendar-decade: early adolescence (the Ultimate dorm-room period), mid-adolescence (the post-incursion 616 integration), and late adolescence (the Ahmed/Ziglar contemporary present). Each phase is treated below at clinical depth, with attention to what *changed*, what *consolidated*, and what *remained latent and unaddressed*. I will also project forward — what the trajectory predicts for the early-twenties Ganke that canon has not yet reached, because a real intelligence file does not stop where the cameras stop.

---

## Phase I — Early Adolescence (ca. age 13, *Ultimate Comics: Spider-Man* 2011 era)

### Affect Regulation

In the dorm-room disclosure sequence (*USM* 2011 #2–4), Ganke's affect under what should be a sympathetic-nervous-system flooding event — his roommate's body sticking to walls, vanishing, electrically discharging — registers as *delight*, *curiosity*, and *cognitive engagement*. This is not numbing or dissociation; it is a phenotype in which **novelty trumps threat appraisal**. The amygdala-mediated fear response is being routed through, or perhaps preempted by, a strongly conditioned approach response to the genre-coded familiar (powers, costume, secret identity). He has spent enough developmental time inside the symbolic universe of superhero narrative that its real-world manifestation reads as **schema confirmation**, not violation. The affective tone is closer to a child unwrapping an anticipated gift than to a witness of the uncanny.

This baseline — *high novelty seeking, low threat reactivity within familiar narrative schemata* — sets the tonal floor for the rest of his life. He does not get rattled by the categorically strange; he gets rattled by the **socially exposing**.

Regulation in this phase is **externalizing-verbal**: he talks his way through arousal. He has not yet developed the layered comedic deflection of later phases; his humor here is more straightforwardly enthusiastic than ironic. When Miles is distraught, Ganke's regulation strategy is to *narrate the situation into manageable shape* — naming it, comparing it to known templates, suggesting concrete next actions. He does not yet have the meta-awareness that this is what he is doing.

The disclosure-leak event with Judge is the phase's defining affective failure. The behavioral evidence indicates not malice but **affective overflow** — the secret, held alone, generated an arousal load that exceeded his thirteen-year-old containment capacity, and he discharged the load through the most available regulatory channel: telling another trusted peer. He framed it post-hoc as utilitarian (Miles needs backup), but the framing reads as **rationalization of an affect-driven act**, a defense in the neurotic-immature range characteristic of early adolescence.

### Cognitive Style

Pattern-saturated, associative, template-driven. He thinks in **genre primitives**: hero, secret identity, costume, sidekick, villain, origin. Confronted with novel data, his first move is to **match-to-template** from the cultural library. This is the developmentally appropriate cognitive strategy of the gifted-hobbyist adolescent — schema-rich, slow to revise schemas, but fast within them.

Working memory and processing speed read as well above peer norm. He follows complex narrative and technical content in real time, code-switches between registers (peer, parent, teacher), and produces the costume recommendation that becomes Miles's identity inside what is, narratively, a single sustained conversation. The cognition is **convergent under enthusiasm** — he funnels rapidly toward concrete recommendation when the affective valence is positive — and **divergent under ambiguity**, generating multiple parallel possibilities when uncertain.

Metacognition is limited. He does not yet examine his own thinking; he just thinks fast.

### Self-Concept

Provisional, role-seeking, not yet consolidated. He has not yet articulated himself as *the guy in the chair*; the role is being lived but not named. Self-evaluation is light, self-deprecation already present but in a buoyant register — he locates himself as not-the-hero without affective weight, because the not-being-the-hero is offset by the **thrilling proximity** to one. His identity in this phase is largely **relationally constructed via Miles** — he is becoming someone through being beside someone becoming someone.

There is no detectable envy substrate. The empirical absence is striking. By Erikson's framework he is mid-Industry-vs-Inferiority with early Identity-vs-Role-Confusion overlay; the standard developmental failure mode in this window for an academically capable child adjacent to a more visibly chosen peer would be *inferiority compensation* (grandiosity, contempt, competitive striving). None appears. The most parsimonious early read is that Ganke's self-worth was already adequately scaffolded by family and academic competence *before* meeting Miles, such that Miles's emergent specialness did not threaten him.

---

## Phase II — Mid-Adolescence (ca. ages 14–15, *Secret Wars* transition through *Spider-Man* 2016)

### Affect Regulation

The phase's central development is the **maturation of humor from enthusiasm to deflection**. The earlier "this is so cool" register persists but is increasingly overlaid with **ironic distance** — the meta-commentary, the pop-culture analog deployed precisely when the affective stakes spike. By Vaillant's defensive hierarchy, this is the migration from immature-neurotic defenses (rationalization, fantasy) toward the mature defense of **humor proper** — the capacity to acknowledge a painful or threatening reality while modulating its sting through wit, *without denying it*. This is one of the most prognostically favorable defensive consolidations available in adolescence.

The body-at-rest, mind-engaged posture also crystallizes in this phase. The horizontal-on-the-bed-with-LEGO baseline is not laziness; it is a **stable autoregulatory configuration** — proprioceptive low arousal (supine, contained), focused fine-motor repetitive activity (building), and ambient social attentiveness (commenting on Miles). It produces a sustained parasympathetic-dominant state from which he can ramp up to engagement and ramp back down without large excursions. He has, without articulating it, **engineered his own optimal regulatory environment**.

Romantic affect — the Bombshell subplot — introduces a new and *unregulated* affective domain. Here the layered defenses thin visibly. He is fumbling, blushing-coded, hyperverbal in the **anxious** rather than the witty mode. The differential matters: in the Miles-domain his verbal output is competent and modulated; in the romantic-domain it is leakage. This indicates the defenses he has built are **domain-specific to the friendship-and-hero-life context** and do not yet generalize.

The chronic stress load increases sharply in this phase as Miles's life pulls him into more dangerous and more public situations. Ganke absorbs the load without symptomatic presentation, which is itself a datum — *either* he is genuinely metabolizing it through the regulatory protocol described above, *or* he is accumulating an unprocessed reserve that the current frame is not yet stressing enough to surface. Both readings are simultaneously true and the relative weighting is the central unanswered psychological question of the file.

### Cognitive Style

The genre-template cognition begins to **stack with systems thinking**. He moves from "this is like a comic" toward "here is the operational architecture of Miles's hero-life and here are its failure modes." He fabricates alibis, runs comms, monitors information environments. The cognition becomes **scenario-planning** in addition to pattern-matching. This is a substantial qualitative shift — from consumer of narrative schemas to **architect of operational ones**.

Metacognition begins to emerge. He starts to notice that he is the one who knows things — that his role has a shape — and to deliberately inhabit it. The self-narration "guy in the chair" begins to function as both job description and identity scaffold.

Cognitive vulnerability sharpens accordingly: the same template-confidence that lets him orient instantly in chaos also predisposes him to **anchor too hard on the wrong template**. When situations diverge from the genre primitives, he can be slow to update.

### Self-Concept
